\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$class RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$\newline
class cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}
\doxylink{struct_hash}{Hash} set based on multi-\/level array, \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_desc}{RCU} specialization 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_container_FeldmanHashSet_rcu}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_container_FeldmanHashSet_rcu}%
 Source\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}2013\mbox{]} Steven Feldman, Pierre La\+Borde, Damian Dechev "{}\+Concurrent Multi-\/level Arrays\+:          Wait-\/free Extensible Hash Maps"{}
\end{DoxyItemize}

See algorithm short description \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_feldman_hash_set_cds_intrusive_FeldmanHashSet_hp}{here}

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Two important things you should keep in mind when you\textquotesingle{}re using {\ttfamily Feldman\+Hash\+Set}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item all keys must be fixed-\/size. It means that you cannot use {\ttfamily std\+::string} as a key for {\ttfamily Feldman\+Hash\+Set}. Instead, for the strings you should use well-\/known hashing algorithms like \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Secure_Hash_Algorithm}{\texttt{ SHA1, SHA2}}, \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MurmurHash}{\texttt{ Murmur\+Hash}}, \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CityHash}{\texttt{ City\+Hash}} or its successor \href{https://code.google.com/p/farmhash/}{\texttt{ Farm\+Hash}} and so on, which converts variable-\/length strings to fixed-\/length bit-\/strings, and use that hash as a key in {\ttfamily Feldman\+Hash\+Set}.
\item {\ttfamily Feldman\+Hash\+Set} uses a perfect hashing. It means that if two different keys, for example, of type {\ttfamily std\+::string}, have identical hash then you cannot insert both that keys in the set. {\ttfamily Feldman\+Hash\+Set} does not maintain the key, it maintains its fixed-\/size hash value.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
The set supports \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_cds_container_FeldmanHashSet_iterators}{bidirectional thread-\/safe iterators}.

Template parameters\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily RCU} -\/ one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type}
\item {\ttfamily T} -\/ a value type to be stored in the set
\item {\ttfamily Traits} -\/ type traits, the structure based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashset_1_1traits}{feldman\+\_\+hashset\+::traits}} or result of {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashset_1_1make__traits}{feldman\+\_\+hashset\+::make\+\_\+traits}} metafunction. {\ttfamily Traits} is the mandatory argument because it has one mandatory type -\/ an \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashset_1_1traits_ae0d4c51659ec6c65556399227ca8e5bb}{accessor} to hash value of {\ttfamily T}. The set algorithm does not calculate that hash value.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Before including {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{intrusive_2feldman__hashset__rcu_8h}{cds/intrusive/feldman\+\_\+hashset\+\_\+rcu.\+h}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} you should include appropriate RCU header file, see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type} for list of existing RCU class and corresponding header files.
\end{DoxyNote}
The set supports \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_container_FeldmanHashSet_rcu_iterators}{bidirectional thread-\/safe iterators} with some restrictions. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

typedef base\+\_\+class\+::iterator \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::iterator}

Bidirectional iterator \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_container_FeldmanHashSet_rcu_iterators}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_container_FeldmanHashSet_rcu_iterators}%
The set supports thread-\/safe iterators\+: you may iterate over the set in multi-\/threaded environment under explicit RCU lock. RCU lock requirement means that inserting or searching is allowed but you must not erase the items from the set since erasing under RCU lock can lead to a deadlock. However, another thread can call {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afa430252ec652a87913255e2c3923803}{erase()}} safely while your thread is iterating.

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} typical example is\+:

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{uint32\_t}}\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{hash}};}

Each iterator object supports the common interface\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item dereference operators\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8420472000570956581ff3ff78bfb619}{value\_type}}\ [\textcolor{keyword}{const}]\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{operator\ -\/>}}()\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{noexcept}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8420472000570956581ff3ff78bfb619}{value\_type}}\ [\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{const}}]\ \&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{operator}}\ *()\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{noexcept}}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item pre-\/increment and pre-\/decrement. Post-\/operators is not supported
\item equality operators {\ttfamily ==} and {\ttfamily !=}. Iterators are equal iff they point to the same cell of the same array node. Note that for two iterators {\ttfamily it1} and {\ttfamily it2} the condition {\ttfamily  it1 == it2 } does not entail {\ttfamily  \&(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}it1) == \&(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}it2) }\+: welcome to concurrent containers
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
It is possible the item can be iterated more that once, for example, if an iterator points to the item in an array node that is being splitted. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_af90583bd4b540dec1175ca03d5263cf5}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!iterator@{iterator}}
\index{iterator@{iterator}!cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{iterator}{iterator}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_af90583bd4b540dec1175ca03d5263cf5} 
typedef base\+\_\+class\+::iterator \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::iterator}



Bidirectional iterator 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_cds_container_FeldmanHashSet_iterators}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_cds_container_FeldmanHashSet_iterators}%
The set supports thread-\/safe iterators\+: you may iterate over the set in multi-\/threaded environment. It is guaranteed that the iterators will remain valid even if another thread deletes the node the iterator points to\+: Hazard Pointer embedded into the iterator object protects the node from physical reclamation.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Since the iterator object contains hazard pointer that is a thread-\/local resource, the iterator should not be passed to another thread.
\end{DoxyNote}
Each iterator object supports the following interface\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item dereference operators\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8420472000570956581ff3ff78bfb619}{value\_type}}\ [\textcolor{keyword}{const}]\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{operator\ -\/>}}()\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{noexcept}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8420472000570956581ff3ff78bfb619}{value\_type}}\ [\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{const}}]\ \&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{operator}}\ *()\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{noexcept}}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item pre-\/increment and pre-\/decrement. Post-\/operators is not supported
\item equality operators {\ttfamily ==} and {\ttfamily !=}. Iterators are equal iff they point to the same cell of the same array node. Note that for two iterators {\ttfamily it1} and {\ttfamily it2}, the conditon {\ttfamily  it1 == it2 } does not entail {\ttfamily  \&(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}it1) == \&(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}it2) }
\item helper member function {\ttfamily release()} that clears internal hazard pointer. After {\ttfamily release()} the iterator points to {\ttfamily nullptr} but it still remain valid\+: further iterating is possible.
\end{DoxyItemize}

During iteration you may safely erase any item from the set; \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_afaaafb57182d7e59ae52471a5acab612}{erase\+\_\+at()} function call doesn\textquotesingle{}t invalidate any iterator. If some iterator points to the item to be erased, that item is not deleted immediately but only after that iterator will be advanced forward or backward.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
It is possible the item can be iterated more that once, for example, if an iterator points to the item in array node that is being splitted. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{level\_statistics@{level\_statistics}!cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{level\_statistics}{level\_statistics}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}

Clears the set (non-\/atomic) 

The function unlink all data node from the set. The function is not atomic but is thread-\/safe. After {\ttfamily clear}() the set may not be empty because another threads may insert items. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_a89d13cdd83a629f0717f351d9469e6a9}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!clear@{clear}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::empty (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Checks if the set is empty 

Emptiness is checked by item counting\+: if item count is zero then the set is empty. Thus, the correct item counting feature is an important part of the set implementation. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_a7107e17c23736e089d1cfb729308225b}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!empty@{empty}}

Deletes the item from the set 

The function searches {\ttfamily hash} in the set, deletes the item found, and returns {\ttfamily true}. If that item is not found the function returns {\ttfamily false}.

RCU should not be locked. The function locks RCU internally. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_a7e1c4e9f3d8cea14c0823c8a1f83589d}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase\+\_\+at (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a282bd08bced98e0415b8b90436e9ae6a}{iterator}} const \&}]{iter}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item pointed by iterator {\ttfamily iter} 

Returns {\ttfamily true} if the operation is successful, {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

The function does not invalidate the iterator, it remains valid and can be used for further traversing. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ab53846d61dc899da96c5cfddfbd99be1}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!extract@{extract}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract()}{extract()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ab53846d61dc899da96c5cfddfbd99be1} 
template$<$class RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a29f3fe5c5ec528e18f803624968a38be}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3a42bddebcae3acf418090716bf3b126}{hash\+\_\+type}} const \&}]{hash}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item with specified {\ttfamily hash} 

The function searches {\ttfamily hash} in the set, unlinks it from the set, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item found. If the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a29f3fe5c5ec528e18f803624968a38be}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked. The function does not call the disposer for the item found. The disposer will be implicitly invoked when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. Example\+:

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract()}{extract()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_a1c63a14b6e2bc8b5b48224f3472f469c} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_ac28813a91b3e98f2e4799a93ee1d7a3c}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3a42bddebcae3acf418090716bf3b126}{hash\+\_\+type}} const \&}]{hash}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item with specified {\ttfamily hash} 

The function searches {\ttfamily hash} in the set, unlinks it from the set, and returns a guarded pointer to the item extracted. If {\ttfamily hash} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

The item returned is reclaimed by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} when returned \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_ac28813a91b3e98f2e4799a93ee1d7a3c}{guarded\+\_\+ptr} object to be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_ac28813a91b3e98f2e4799a93ee1d7a3c}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

template$<$typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::find (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3a42bddebcae3acf418090716bf3b126}{hash\+\_\+type}} const \&}]{hash}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds an item by it\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily hash} 

The function searches the item by {\ttfamily hash} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found.

The functor may change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. Note that the functor is only guarantee that {\ttfamily item} cannot be disposed during the functor is executing. The functor does not serialize simultaneous access to the set\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema on item level to prevent unsafe item modifications.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily hash} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. 函数调用图\+:

Finds an item by it\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily hash} and returns the item found 

The function searches the item by its {\ttfamily hash} and returns the pointer to the item found. If {\ttfamily hash} is not found the function returns {\ttfamily nullptr}.

RCU should be locked before the function invocation. Returned pointer is valid only while RCU is locked.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_ac28813a91b3e98f2e4799a93ee1d7a3c}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses one GC\textquotesingle{}s guard which can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+level\+\_\+statistics (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashset_a53ccc7bd7719d07a866a4cbcc78e9f1e}{feldman\+\_\+hashset\+::level\+\_\+statistics}} $>$ \&}]{stat}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Collects tree level statistics into {\ttfamily stat} 

The function traverses the set and collects statistics for each level of the tree into {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashset_a53ccc7bd7719d07a866a4cbcc78e9f1e}{feldman\+\_\+hashset\+::level\+\_\+statistics}} struct. The element of {\ttfamily stat}\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} represents statistics for level {\ttfamily i}, level 0 is head array. The function is thread-\/safe and may be called in multi-\/threaded environment.

Result can be useful for estimating efficiency of hash functor you use. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_a101f9c62ba5b4bf8a0af582144384643}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!get\_level\_statistics@{get\_level\_statistics}}
\index{get\_level\_statistics@{get\_level\_statistics}!cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_level\_statistics()}{get\_level\_statistics()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_a101f9c62ba5b4bf8a0af582144384643}

Collects tree level statistics into {\ttfamily stat} 

The function traverses the set and collects statistics for each level of the tree into {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashset_a53ccc7bd7719d07a866a4cbcc78e9f1e}{feldman\+\_\+hashset\+::level\+\_\+statistics}} struct. The element of {\ttfamily stat}\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} represents statistics for level {\ttfamily i}, level 0 is head array. \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new element 

The function creates an element with copy of {\ttfamily val} value and then inserts it into the set.

The type {\ttfamily Q} should contain as minimum the complete hash for the element. The object of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8420472000570956581ff3ff78bfb619}{value\+\_\+type} should be constructible from a value of type {\ttfamily Q}. In trivial case, {\ttfamily Q} is equal to \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8420472000570956581ff3ff78bfb619}{value\+\_\+type}.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set, {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

The function locks RCU internally. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_a278d92869523f6e94066ee585e4ec47a}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ac26fc16f6d3418a30dd1563224bbe1bf} 
template$<$class RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new element 

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the set
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/fields of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8420472000570956581ff3ff78bfb619}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. User-\/defined functor {\ttfamily f} should guarantee that during changing {\ttfamily val} no any other changes could be made on this set\textquotesingle{}s item by concurrent threads. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success.

The function locks RCU internally. 函数调用图\+:

\index{update@{update}!cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update()}{update()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae13994efee57c59e1e048199f7247d83} 
template$<$class RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Func$>$ \\
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the element 

The operation performs inserting or replacing with lock-\/free manner.

If the {\ttfamily val} key not found in the set, then the new item created from {\ttfamily val} will be inserted into the set iff {\ttfamily b\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, if {\ttfamily val} is found, it is replaced with new item created from {\ttfamily val} and previous item is disposed. In both cases {\ttfamily func} functor is called.

The functor {\ttfamily Func} signature\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{my\_functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cur}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{value\_type}}\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{prev}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily cur} -\/ current element
\item {\ttfamily prev} -\/ pointer to previous element with such hash. {\ttfamily prev} is {\ttfamily nullptr} if {\ttfamily cur} was just inserted.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}; however, {\ttfamily func} must guarantee that during changing no any other modifications could be made on this item by concurrent threads.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, i.\+e. the item has been inserted or updated, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if the new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with key equal to {\ttfamily val} already exists. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_ad01714c11e3d816bf7b37580ec417517}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!update@{update}}
\index{update@{update}!cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update()}{update()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set_ad01714c11e3d816bf7b37580ec417517} 
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the element 

The operation performs inserting or replacing with lock-\/free manner.

If the {\ttfamily val} key not found in the set, then the new item created from {\ttfamily val} will be inserted into the set iff {\ttfamily b\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, if {\ttfamily val} is found, it is replaced with new item created from {\ttfamily val} and previous item is disposed. In both cases {\ttfamily func} functor is called.

The functor {\ttfamily Func} signature\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{my\_functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{cur}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{value\_type}}\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_set}{prev}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily cur} -\/ current element
\item {\ttfamily prev} -\/ pointer to previous element with such hash. {\ttfamily prev} is {\ttfamily nullptr} if {\ttfamily cur} was just inserted.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}; however, {\ttfamily func} must guarantee that during changing no any other modifications could be made on this item by concurrent threads.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, i.\+e. the item has been inserted or updated, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if the new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with key equal to {\ttfamily val} already exists.
